experienced, and make going there feel like you are in another world. They wait on you hand and
foot. If you are in a hurry they have two operaters servicing you.

I have gone 15 minutes before closing and without any hesitation they sit you down turn the massage chair on and get right to work. One doing the
mani the other the pedi but never

<userid>110835274214414477505</userid><username>Y√º Wu<//username><Time>1618964936895<//Time><rating>4<//rating>< text>
Sunny and clean city park with a nice lawn, dog area and a small beach! I passed by the park during a run along the coast and enjoyed a little stop in this beautiful park. There are some picnic tables in the park which is awesome but otherwise there aren't a lot of facilities in the park so I think it has some potentials to be more interesting.
The neighborhood feels modern and urban, has plenty of restaurants and cafes within a short walk.< /text>

The Bartlett Hotel and guesthouse is great inexpensive place well located as a launching point for visiting the city. My deluxe room with a private bathroom (Including a tub/shower) was clean, light and airy with large windows. The staff(Susan) was most welcoming and helpful throughout my 3 day stay. I would definitely stay here again. On the second floor is a full kitchen for cooking my own meals if I like. And coin operated washers and dryers. Filtered water dispenser.</Text>

< name>
Dennis Ginsig<//name>
<Date>1553984689862</Date><rate>3< /rate>< text>
This hotel is very basic overall. Design is not bad, the amenities do work just well enough and staff was not always friendly but helpful. Don't expect much, it will do the job:

The first room I got had only one window; and it faced a concrete wall. Staff was kind enough to find me another room for my remaining nights though.

My room was not serviced every day even though I asked for it at the check-in and put up a "make up my room" sign.

Shower was hard to figure out and more of a tepid drizzle.

No extras such as toothbrush or hairdryer.

In summation, I think it's fair to say that the hotel was ok but a bit on the expensive side for what it delivers.</text>

<date>1618251478427<//date><Pics>None</Pics><Resp>None</Resp><username>Heleina Carnovale</username><rate>5< /rate><user>110113358727892126209< /user><gmap_id>0x8085808f15d54abd:0xf312c0cb03577779</gmap_id>< text>
I see some reviews that felt the hotel was lackluster. It may be lacking in a few amenities that other larger hotels have. Was relocated from the sister property The Herbert, which I was initially upset about.  However, it is a very cute old narrow building in the heart of Union Square. Close to major bus routes, BART and attractions. Felt very safe here, given it is downtown and the Tenderloin is just a few blocks away. Double key-pad entry plus the need for a key to use the elevator. I felt safe here at night with my two children. They thought the rooms were cute and liked our view from the 6th floor. I believe there are 7 floors. I love the rooms and thought it had an old New York apartment feel to it. However, one elevator and it is small. Other than that, I enjoyed my stay here.<//text>

< text>
I stayed July 2019 in the private queen room and it was exactly like  the photos, cute, clean, comfy bed and a nice clean bathroom. We were looking for a budget friendly option and this was definitely a good hotel for the price. The only issue we had was the lift broke when we arrived (we had to take our bags up some steep/narrow stairs) but the staff made sure it got fixed the next day. There is a bistro/bar next door which was great for quick easy meals on some of the nights we were exhausted and just wanted to eat and crash (also good options for breakfast). The area itself is busy and very close to the Bart station however it can be a slightly shady area. Neither of us felt comfortable walking around at night (felt fine during the day) however that might also be us not being used to the overall atmosphere of the Tenderloin. Overall if budget is your main concern and you are looking for the best bang for your buck this is a simple, cute and cosy private hotel room perfect for a few days in SF.< /text>

No luggage service was provided (even with the elevator out of service) and if your room was not ready upon arrival you would be charged $2/hr for the front desk to hold your luggage. Bed comfort was less than optimal as was the temperature control of the room. Even after placing a please provide service tag on our room door our room was not cleaned for 3 days. The only day housekeeping cleaned was the first day and upon our return from a day in the city there were NO towels or wash rags in our room. When we requested clean towels from the front desk in person we were met with rudeness, eye rolling, and a response of "Do you need them now?" For the lack of service provided by this establishment the cost should have been less than half of what was charged and they should be advertised as a dormitory or hostel not a hotel.</review>

< Text>
Pros: We were happy with the room itself - nothing fancy, but since we were more interested in exploring the city, it was fine. It was also very quiet, since our windows faced a closed alley. The restaurant/bar downstairs has a good happy hour and the food was pretty good.

Cons: One of the windows didn't have a safety block to prevent it opening all the way; dangerous, given that we were on the 5th floor. The staircase was narrow and poorly-lit. The elevator was cramped, rickety, and didn't always feel like it stopped completely before the door opened. Generally, the building did not feel like it would meet fire codes and the shared spaces were more akin to what I've seen in poorly-maintained hostels.

Worst of all, on the first night, my partner starting feeling dizzy and nauseous after standing next to the open window. (We kept the windows open bc there is no AC.) Since he had been ill earlier in the week, we didn't think anything of it. However, on the third night, we both started having the same symptoms almost immediately after entering the room. We had been feeling fine all day and this was an abrupt change. After still no improvement from showering, we went back down to street level and reported this to the front desk, who didn't seem too concerned nor surprised. They said that although it wasn't frequent, this wasn't the first time this had been reported and asked if we smelled any "cleaning agents". We hadn't.

After spending a little time downstairs, the fresh air began to alleviate the issues but we weren't convinced we would be comfortable nor safe in our room. As a possible solution, the hotel staff offered to move us to a different room and gave us the key to check it out first. We went to the room (two floors up from our original room, facing the street instead of the alley), but we didn't feel better/started to feel the symptoms again. It was at this point that we decided we didn't feel safe, especially considering that our symptoms were among those listed for carbon monoxide poisoning and this wasn't the first time the hotel staff had heard this kind of issue from guests. We checked out and went to another hotel nearby.

Although we were refunded the nights remaining on our prepaid reservation, this whole experience was very disruptive to our trip and due to the last minute change, we ended up spending much more on lodging than expected.< /Text>

<username>Chak Long 'Chris' Cheung</username>< Text>
Location is good, downtown and surrounded by everything you would need (Walgreens, Starbucks, Chipotle, Trader Joe's, etc. all within walking distance). Walking distance from public transit. Entrance was difficult to find, and the building itself is very rudimentary, with fairly thin walls and doors, along with a slow and very basic elevator. Room was perfectly adequate for me, everything was clean, and there was a single table attached to the wall that I could work on, although it was slightly loose and slanted. There was also a television that I didn't use. Bathroom was well stocked with shampoo, towels, etc. Nothing else to really talk about. Front desk was friendly and helpful, checked-in past midnight and had no issues with staff. Wi-Fi worked perfectly for my light internet use, but definitely not sufficient for anything more than that. Basic and adequate. However, walls and doors seem paper thin, could clearly hear noise from the hallway.<//Text>

room
